The lights are dimmed, the projector is off, and the air smells like **old coffee, printer toner, and stress sweat**.  **Cremeans** sits slouched in a chair, laptop open, three energy drinks deep, bags under his eyes like bruises. His fingers move slowly, methodically.

**CREMEANS (dry, almost slurring)**  
Does anyone realize…that **Madeline had four hundred and twelve alt accounts** on Twitter?

**JEFF (without looking up)**  
Elon doesn’t like it when you call it Twitter.  It’s **X**.

**JEREMY (snaps up from his chair, bloodshot)**  
*Elon doesn’t like it—Elon doesn’t like it—*

**JEREMY (exploding)**  
*Shut the fuck up, Jeff.*  It’s called **Twitter**, you son of a bitch.  *You grew up in Ohio, not Mars.*

**Under the table, a foot kicks hard against the wood.**  The whole thing shudders.

**SARAH (muffled, deadly)**  
Would you *please* shut the hell up so I can get **thirty goddamn minutes** of sleep?

Silence.

**CREMEANS (without missing a beat, still typing)**  
I’ve got **fifty-three variations** of the message rolling.  Some with hashtags. Some without.  Some pushing the victim angle. Some pushing mental health.  A couple pulling the “music family” card.

He yawns mid-sentence, stretches his jaw.

**CREMEANS (checking his screen)**  
It’ll take… four to five hours to reach saturation.  Maybe three if we get a boost from one of our verifieds.

**SARAH (groaning under the table)**  
Wake me when it's trending.

**JEFF (quietly)**  
We’re all going to die in this room, aren’t we?

**JEREMY (shrugging)**  
Not before we hit the New York Times front page.

**Cremeans sips from a half-flat Diet Coke.**

**CREMEANS**  
You’re welcome.

---

### **SCENE: “Page One” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MIDNIGHT THIRTY**

**Cremeans** refreshes the browser for the **seventeenth time** in ten minutes, eyes twitching.

**F5. F5. F5.**

And then—

**CREMEANS (flat, triumphant)**  
*Boom.*

Everyone looks up.

**CREMEANS (leans back, pointing at the screen)**  
**Avril.** Page one. **New York Times.**  Fifth slot.

He squints.

**CREMEANS (reading aloud)**  
Right under: *“Trump Clinches Ohio in 2024 GOP Primary.”*

**JEREMY (rubbing his face, deadpan)**  
I think that orange bastard might actually win this sucker.

**From under the conference table—**

**SARAH (growls)**  
*No fucking politics.*

**Beat.**

**SARAH (louder)**  
*Let me sleep, you sons of bitches.*

**JEFF (muttering)**  
I miss when we just made music.

**JEREMY (grins)**  
Yeah, remember when the biggest drama was someone leaking a demo?

**CREMEANS (clicking again)**  
Now we leak *narratives*.  Fifty-three and counting.

**SARAH (still muffled)**  
Fifty-four if you don’t shut up.

**Silence.**

A truck honks outside.  Someone’s phone buzzes and no one even flinches.  They just sit there… waiting for the next fire to catch.

---

### **SCENE: “Toxicology” – Island Records, Conference Room / Bennett’s Office / NYPD Forensics**

**INT. SECURE LOCATION – EARLY MORNING**

A **fax machine hums.**  A report slides through.  Across multiple screens, across offices and phones and eyes, the **toxicology and forensic findings** arrive.

**BENNETT KING**, alone in a downtown suite, reads the summary out loud to himself — flat, focused, and as cold as the data.

**BENNETT (reading)**  
Blood Alcohol Content: 0.23.  Above motor impairment. Borderline alcohol poisoning. Lethal range.

**He flips a page. Eyes narrowing.**

**BENNETT**  
Methamphetamine: Present.  
Amphetamine: Present.  
Cocaine: Present.  
Poly-drug interaction likely. Stimulant overload. Agitation, euphoria, psychosis risk… all elevated.

**A beat. The page turns again.**

**BENNETT (more quietly)**  
Semen detected… *in the stomach.*

**He stops reading for a beat. Processes it.**

**BENNETT (resumes, flatter)**  
Three unique semen samples identified from vaginal swabs.  None match each other.  None are currently in the system.

**Page turn.**

**BENNETT**  
Semen found on outer shirt — not matching any internal samples.

**Page turn.**

**BENNETT**  
Underwear tested positive for biological material from at least two additional donors.

**He sets the paper down. Doesn’t speak.**

**INT. ISLAND RECORDS – CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

**Cremeans**, **Jeremy**, and **Sarah** are staring at their phones. The reports are now in everyone’s inbox.

No one says anything.

**JEREMY (quietly)**  
That’s five.

**CREMEANS (dead whisper)**  
Five… different men.  And one in the stomach.

**SARAH (slowly rising from under the table, voice like stone)**  
That’s not a spiral.

**She looks up.**

**SARAH**  
That’s a fucking implosion.

---

### **SCENE: “Fighting Words” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – DAWN**

The air is thick with dread. The **toxicology report** lies open on the table, untouched now. No one speaks for a long beat.

Then:

**JEFF (quiet, stunned)**  
Then how the hell do we fix this?

**BILL (cold, muttering)**  
We don’t.  We never should’ve brought her on board in the first place.

**JEFF (snaps his head up)**  
*What did you just say?*

**BILL (shrugs)**  
You heard me.

**JEFF (getting up, voice rising)**  
You’re gonna apologize for that, *right now*…

**He grabs a chair — not swinging it, but *gripping it*** — the room shifts with tension.

**JEFF**  
Or I swear to God, I’m gonna see just how far I can shove this *up your goddamn ass*.

**BILL (snorts, rising too)**  
That’s it? That’s your line?  *Those are fighting words?*

He steps in, chest out.

**BILL (mocking)**  
You don’t look like you’re gonna back that up, there… *pussy*.

**JEFF (roars)**  
*Say it again\!*

**JEREMY (stepping in between them)**  
*HEY\!*

**He puts a hand on Jeff’s chest, the other raised toward Bill.**

**JEREMY**  
*Back off — both of you\!*

**CREMEANS (from the corner, eyes hollow)**  
Guys, not now. Not with this shit hanging in the air.

**SARAH (dead serious, stepping forward slowly)**  
If either of you break anything in this room —  chairs, faces, bones, reputations —  I *swear to God*, I’ll bury you both in NDAs and lawsuits so deep you'll need mining gear to get out.

**Silence.**

**Jeff’s hands are shaking. Bill’s jaw is clenched.**  But neither moves.  Just the low hum of city noise outside.

**JEFF (quieter, staring at Bill)**  
You don’t get to talk about her like that.  Not after what she’s been through.

**BILL (gruff)**  
Then maybe someone should’ve protected her better.

**JEFF (low)**  
We’re trying to.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Hell on Earth” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – JUST AFTER DAWN**

Tension still radiates from the fight that almost happened. The room is frozen in silence — and then **Bill explodes.**

**BILL (shouting)**  
*You all don’t get it.*

He steps back from the table like it’s radioactive, fists clenched, breathing ragged.

**BILL (yelling)**  
You *haven’t seen it*. You haven’t *smelled* it.

**He points at each of them, eyes wild.**

**BILL**  
I went down into a **drug den** three stories beneath this goddamn city.  No light. No exit. No cell service.

**He slams his hand on the table. Hard.**

**BILL (furious, shaking)**  
It was *hell on fucking earth*.  And *the rats* — the rats were circling her.

**Beat.**

**BILL (voice cracking)**  
They were gonna *eat her*.

The words hang in the air like poison.

**BILL**  
Thirty seconds later? She’d have been *shredded*.  An hour? *Corpse.* Nothing left but bones and press coverage.

**No one speaks.**

**BILL (quieter, shaking with adrenaline)**  
And I had to carry her **heavy, limp body** up *three flights of stairs in the dark*.  No elevator. No backup. Just *me* and a girl who was barely breathing.

**He looks up, eyes rimmed red.**

**BILL (dead cold)**  
And you know what happened next?

**He doesn’t wait.**

**BILL (bitter)**  
NYPD threw me in the back of a cop car.  Didn’t ask. Didn’t listen. Just cuffed me and threw me in like I was the piece of shit who *left her down there*.

**He points around the room, voice shaking with fury.**

**BILL**  
So if anyone here wants to talk about “fixing this” or “protecting the brand” or “what we should’ve done” —

**He grabs a nearby coffee cup and hurls it into the trash. Hard.**

**BILL (final)**  
You can all just *fuck right off.*

**Silence. Deafening.**  **Cremeans** slowly lowers his laptop screen.  **Sarah**, under the table still, says nothing.  **Jeff**, for once, doesn't fire back.  Because now they’ve heard it.  **Not the PR version. Not the news headline.**  *The real thing.*

---

# **“Ohio Arrival” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. ISLAND RECORDS – CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

**DING.**

The **elevator chimes**.

The glass doors slide open and in steps **Jim**, suitcase in one hand, messenger bag over his shoulder, looking like he just got off a **Delta flight and a good night’s sleep**.

He beams.

**JIM (cheerful)**  
Hey, hey, team. *Miss me?*

No one answers.  **Jim** pauses mid-stride. The conference room looks like the aftermath of a riot.  Chairs are sideways. Coffee cups everywhere.  Cremeans is pale and blinking like a lizard.  Sarah is basking under the conference table.  Bill is vibrating with rage.  Jeremy and Jeff are half-standing, like they’re still deciding if a fight is going to happen.

**JIM (uncertain now)**  
…Wow.  Okay.  So… is now a bad time to ask for an update?

**SARAH (from under the table)**  
Only if you want to keep your dick.

**CREMEANS (flat)**  
Welcome to *hell*, Jim.

**JIM (still too chipper)**  
O-kay! That’s… helpful.

**He sets down his suitcase and claps once, awkwardly.**

**JIM (forced optimism)**  
So… what’s the game plan?  PR? Legal? Do we have a crisis board or—

**JEFF (cutting in, exhausted)**  
You want a board?  Grab a marker and draw one in blood.

**BILL (snaps)**  
*Shut up, Jeff.*

**JIM (finally catching on)**  
Right. Got it.  Reading the room.  Bad vibes.

**He pulls out a folding chair and sits… way too straight.**

**JIM (softer now)**  
Okay. So seriously.  Can someone catch me up before the sun explodes?

---

### **SCENE: “The Hug” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – CONTINUOUS**

The elevator door slides open again.  This time, no chime. No announcement.  **Madeline Quinlan** walks in.  She’s still in the same clothes. Her hair’s clean, barely. Her eyes are hollow. Her expression is **stone**.

She doesn’t say a word.  She crosses the room slowly, like every step hurts more than the last, and lowers herself into a chair that’s too big, too official, too cold.  She just sits.  And **sulks.**  Quiet.  Not angry — just **emptied out**.

Everyone freezes.  Even **Jim** stays silent.  Then—**Bill** turns and **looks at her.**  Really looks.  And for a long beat, it seems like he’s going to say something. Maybe something snide. Maybe nothing at all.

But instead?

He walks across the room.  And without a word… **he hugs her.**  A full-body, no-performance, arms-around-the-shoulders **human hug.**  **Madeline tenses**—shocked—but doesn’t pull away.  She just… **lets it happen**.

**Jeremy’s mouth falls open slightly.**  **Jeff looks down at the floor.**  
**Sarah shifts under the table and watches, silent.**  **Cremeans** just nods once, barely noticeable, like it makes sense now.

**No one says anything.**  Because for once?  There’s **nothing to spin.**  Just a girl who almost died.  And a man who carried her out of hell.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Reward” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

The hug ends.

**Bill** steps back, nods once.  **Madeline** doesn’t look up.  Silence swells around her — everyone watching, waiting.  Then she speaks.

**MADELINE (quietly, without looking at anyone)**  
I did my job.

**No one moves.**

**MADELINE (still soft)**  
I did it well.

**She finally looks up, eyes glassy but steady.**

**MADELINE**  
And they gave me a **body cavity search** as a reward.

Silence.

Thick. Awful. No one knows where to put their eyes.

**Jeremy shifts uncomfortably.**  **Cremeans stares at his laptop like he’s hoping it will rescue him.**  **Jim looks like he’s trying to shrink into his chair.**  **Sarah closes her eyes.**

But **no one speaks**.  Because **what could they possibly say**?

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “A Word” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

Silence after Madeline’s line. Stillness. The kind that cuts.

**Cremeans** sits hunched at the table, fingers twitching, eyes flicking between tabs on his laptop, the search bar already half-full of a verse he barely remembers but desperately needs.

**He mutters to himself.**  
“Come on, come on…”

Then he finds it.

**CREMEANS (quietly, clearing his throat)**  
Uh…

Everyone glances at him — even Madeline, slowly.

He looks directly at her, voice soft and worn.

**CREMEANS**  
*"We are hard pressed on every side, but not crushed;*  
*perplexed, but not in despair;*  
*persecuted, but not abandoned;*  
*struck down, but not destroyed."*

**He swallows.**

**CREMEANS**  
Second Corinthians. Chapter four.

Madeline stares at him, stunned for a moment — like it just hit her **he noticed**.

She doesn’t say thank you.  She doesn’t need to.

**Everyone else looks down.**  **The words just… settle in.**

Bill nods, slowly.  Sarah exhales under the table.  Jeremy closes his eyes.  Because maybe that’s the first time anyone in the room said out loud:  **She’s still here.**

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “You Don’t Know Half of It” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – CONTINUOUS**

Cremeans’ verse still lingers in the air like incense — quiet, heavy, comforting.

**No one speaks.**

Then, from the corner of the room:

**JIM (under his breath)**  
It’s gonna be one of those mornings, isn’t it?

**JEFF (without even turning, voice like gravel)**  
*You don’t know half of it.*

**A beat.**

**Jeremy** lets out a low, bitter chuckle.  **Bill** rubs his face like he’s trying to wake up from a dream.  **Sarah**, still beneath the table, mutters something unintelligible that sounds vaguely like *“coffee or murder”*.

And in that moment, for just a second—**They’re not enemies.**  **Not executives.**  **Not broken people.**Just **a team**, in the middle of the worst day of their lives.  And somehow… **still in it together**.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Triage” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

Silence again. The storm is shifting into fog. Everyone looks shattered — in body, in spirit, in voice.

**Jim** scans the room, sizing up the wreckage. Everyone looks like they’ve survived a small war. In a way, they have.

**JIM (gently)**  
Alright. Maybe I should take **media inquiries** for now.  The **Japanese** and **South Koreans** are already rolling live coverage. Their breakfast shows are about to spin this mess into next Tuesday.

**He grabs his laptop and phone, already pulling up translation plugins and scheduler apps.**

**JIM (nodding to the room)**  
And since y’all look like **a bunch of walking dead**, maybe just… I don’t know…

**He gestures broadly.**

**JIM**  
Pick a **couch**, find a **chair**, crawl under a **table**, hell, grab a **closet** if it’s dark and quiet.  Just **chill**. You’ve earned it. Even your eyeballs look tired.

**He pauses.**

**JIM**  
What time’s the lawyer getting here again?

**JEFF (groggy, eyes barely open)**  
*Five.*

**JIM (half-whistles)**  
AM?

**JEFF**  
Yeah.  Emergency session.  He’s smart enough to get a hotel.

**JIM (muttering)**  
I sure as hell wouldn’t walk into this mess without one.

**SARAH (from under the table)**  
No one walks out of this mess, either.

**JIM**  
Not without a body bag or a Pulitzer.

---

# **"We Have Met the Enemy… ” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – MOMENTS LATER**

**Jim** adjusts his collar, ties his hair back, and sets up his Zoom lighting. He opens his laptop to the NHK waiting room.

**JIM (quietly to himself)**  
Alright, NHK.  Polite. Formal.  Also once asked me if Justin Bieber was a reincarnated Shinto fox spirit.

He exhales.

**JIM (muttering)**  
Polite… but *feral*.

The **Zoom chime dings.** The reporter is in the waiting room.

**JIM (composing himself)**  
Let’s go.

He clicks “Admit.”

**ON SCREEN:**  
A stern-looking NHK anchor in a crisp blue blazer bows deeply from a pristine Tokyo newsroom. Behind him: a graphic of Avril Lavigne, the New York City skyline, and the words in kanji that translate roughly to **“The Scandal of the Soul.”**

**JIM (smiling tightly)**  
Good morning, Takahashi-san. Thank you for reaching out. I’m available to provide a statement and clarification on behalf of the team.

**TAKAHASHI (bowing again)**  
Thank you, Jim-san. It is our honor. We understand this is a time of great spiritual misalignment and possible emotional corrosion. We appreciate your presence.

**Jim freezes for half a second.**

**JIM (blinking, recovering)**  
Yes… It’s, uh, it’s been a challenging moment for the band and our label.

**TAKAHASHI (smiling serenely)**  
Indeed. May I ask—  
*Was Ms. Lavigne acting under the influence of an intoxicating demonic principle?*

**JIM (under his breath)**  
Here we fucking go.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Exquisite Torture” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – LATER**

**Jim’s shirt is rumpled now. His smile? Fractured at the corners.** The NHK interview is still going, now deep into its second hour.

On-screen, **Takahashi** hasn’t blinked once.

**TAKAHASHI (gently, in perfect English)**  
To clarify, Jim-san:  When Ms. Lavigne was discovered in the disused subway facility —  was her exposure to *feral rats* symbolic of a broader American cultural disassociation with purity?

**Jim blinks. Twice.**

**JIM (strained smile)**  
I… I don’t think purity was the primary concern at that point, Takahashi-san. We were focused on *survival.*

**TAKAHASHI (nods gravely)**  
Yes. Survival.  And semen.

**Jim freezes.**

**JIM**  
Sorry?

**TAKAHASHI (reading notes)**  
Our agency has confirmed multiple reports of biological samples, including *semen in the stomach*.  Would you describe this as a spiritual absorption of male shame?

**Jim stares.**

**JIM (to himself, very softly)**  
This would make a fantastic Farrelly Brothers movie if I wasn’t starring in it.

**TAKAHASHI (smiling politely)**  
We are grateful for your transparency.

**JIM (deadpan)**  
I’m not.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Game Changer” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:17 A.M.**

**Jim’s still live.** The NHK anchor’s serene expression hasn’t shifted in the slightest, even as he raises a hand in that gentle, “and now, something new” posture.

**TAKAHASHI (with a slight smile)**  
Jim-san, we thank you for your patience and your graciousness under pressure.

**JIM (half-delirious)**  
Of course. It’s a privilege.

**TAKAHASHI (with gravity)**  
We have received exclusive footage, aired first in our domestic morning broadcast.

**Jim’s eyes narrow.**

**TAKAHASHI (continuing, calmly)**  
It appears to show Ms. Lavigne entering the subway structure—  unaided, uncoerced, and alone.

**Jim stops breathing for half a second.**

**JIM**  
I'm sorry… What?

**TAKAHASHI (bowing slightly)**  
It was captured on private surveillance equipment installed by an urban exploration collective.  The footage has been authenticated.  We are airing it now on our Tokyo feed.

**ON JIM'S LAPTOP** — the corner of the screen shows **grainy, low-light video**:  A solitary figure in black, walking briskly down a maintenance stairwell, disappearing into shadow.

**JIM (barely audible)**  
Son of a bitch.

**TAKAHASHI (smiling, perfectly composed)**  
This changes the frame, does it not?

**Jim swallows hard.**

**JIM (quietly, because it’s live)**  
Yeah.  Yeah, Takahashi-san.  It sure as hell does.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Live Reaction” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – LIVE ON NHK BROADCAST – 2:21 A.M.**

The grainy footage plays in the corner of the screen. The NHK anchor remains composed, watching Jim with the curiosity of someone who *already knows how bad this is going to get.*

**Jim** stares at the monitor for a beat, *processing*, swallowing hard — then turns back toward the camera.

**JIM (clears throat)**  
This is… uh… this is **news to me**.

**He holds up both hands, briefly.**

**JIM (measured)**  
Let me be very clear —  I have never seen this footage before.  I am as shocked and surprised as you are, Takahashi-san, and as, I imagine, your viewers are.

**The anchor nods silently.**

**JIM (deep breath)**  
Obviously, this new footage will require a thorough review.  We’re committed to transparency, but we are also committed to **truth**.  There is context we do not yet have.  And I cannot, and will not, make assumptions live on air.

**He softens his tone now, leaning forward slightly.**

**JIM (sincerely)**  
I would respectfully ask that your audience — and our global viewers — recognize the **gravity of the situation**.

**Beat.**

**JIM**  
We are dealing with a young woman in crisis.  Someone who has been through **a trauma** that is still unfolding hour by hour.

**JIM (steady)**  
So I request, in good faith—  Your **thoughts**, your **prayers**, and most importantly,  your **respect** for Avril’s **privacy** in this moment.

**He nods, once.**

**JIM (quietly)**  
She needs space.  She needs grace.

**The anchor bows slowly in response.**

**TAKAHASHI**  
Beautifully said, Jim-san.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Even Monkeys Fall” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – LIVE BROADCAST – MOMENTS LATER**

Jim gives a soft, composed nod as the NHK anchor bows in response to his appeal for privacy and compassion.

There’s a beat of quiet — and then Jim leans forward, folding his hands neatly, voice low and clear.

**JIM (gently)**  
As we say — *Saru mo ki kara ochiru.*

**Even the monkey falls from the tree.**

**A pause. The NHK anchor tilts his head, visibly impressed.**

**JIM (continuing)**  
No one climbs forever.  No one stays perfect.  Not in music. Not in life. Not in crisis.

He offers the smallest, most exhausted smile of the entire broadcast.

**JIM**  
We fall.  But we try to catch each other on the way down.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “The Sign-Off” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:29 A.M.**

Jim breathes out slowly, hands folded, the faint trace of his Midwestern politeness hanging on by threads. He waits.

Across the screen, **Takahashi** bows deeply, hands neatly folded before him.

**TAKAHASHI (with poise)**  
Jim-san. On behalf of NHK and our viewers,  we thank you for your candor… your composure… and your time.

**He straightens with that same unreadable, serene face.**

**TAKAHASHI**  
This is a moment of great visibility, and we are grateful for your guidance in such delicate cultural terrain.

**JIM (matching the formality)**  
Thank you, Takahashi-san.  It’s been… enlightening.

**TAKAHASHI (bowing once more)**  
May your team find peace.  And may Ms. Lavigne find light in her darkness.

**The call ends.**

**Jim stares at the blank screen for a long moment.**  
Then reaches off-camera and slowly **kills the ring light.**

Darkness.

**JIM (to himself)**  
I'm going to need so much therapy.

---

### **SCENE: “Five Minutes” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – MOMENTS AFTER NHK SIGN-OFF**

The **ring light is off**. The room is dark except for the bluish laptop glow.

**Jim**, still in his chair, leans forward and starts gently **tapping his forehead against the table**.

*Thunk.*  
*Thunk.*  
*Thunk.*

Not hard. Not painful.  Just enough to express: *“Dear God, I am so done.”*

**JIM (muttering into the desk)**  
This is fine.  Everything’s fine.  This is my life now.

**Thunk. Thunk.**

He sits up, exhales.

**JIM (flatly)**  
I gotta get something to drink.

He looks around. There’s a **bottle of Coke Zero** and a **half-empty LaCroix**. He picks up both, considers mixing them, reconsiders.

**JIM**  
Because the **Koreans are next**…

**He checks his watch.**

**JIM (grimacing)**  
And I’ve got **five minutes** to reset my soul.

**He stands. Stretches. Rolls his neck like a boxer about to walk back into the ring.**

**JIM (sighs, to himself)**  
Okay, Seoul.  Bring the thunder.

---

### **SCENE: “Round Two” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – MOMENTS LATER**

The **Zoom window is open.** A South Korean broadcaster’s logo spins slowly on screen. A new anchor is logging in — younger, sharper, already adjusting his mic like he's about to call a UFC fight.

**Jim** slaps his cheeks lightly. Rolls his shoulders.  
**He’s live in 5… 4… 3…**

And in his head—

**JIM (inner monologue, dry as dust)**  
Alright. Here we go.  Everyone knows the **Koreans** are the **gruff, less polite**, and **totally insane younger brothers** to the Japanese.

**2…**

**JIM (inner voice)**  
But if you ever *called* them the **West Virginia of Asia**—

**1…**

**JIM (deadpan thought)**  
—they’d *punch you in the throat* and **piss on your head**.

**LIVE FEED ENGAGES.**

A **Korean SBS anchor** appears instantly — zero preamble, no smiles, eyes already narrowing.

**ANCHOR (blunt)**  
Jim-ssi. Did she take the drugs willingly or was she raped by an entire basketball team?

**Jim blinks once.**

**JIM (aloud, calm)**  
Good morning, and thank you for having me.

**JIM (in his head)**  
*And we’re off to the fucking races.*

**This is war. Again.** And Jim?  **Is out of water and out of grace.**

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Baal-seo-jee-What?” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:41 A.M. – SBS LIVE BROADCAST, SOUTH KOREA**

**Jim** is blinking at the screen like a war survivor. The Korean anchor just asked him if Avril was gang-raped in a meth dungeon. Live. No commercial break. No apology.

**Jim swallows. Hard.**

**JIM (exhausted, smiling faintly)**  
Uh… I…

**He clears his throat, leans in, and tries.**

**JIM (butchering)**  
*Baal… seo… jee-bae-ga… go… sip-yo?*

**A beat. The anchor pauses.**

**ANCHOR (blinks slowly)**  
…Excuse me?

**JIM (rushed, correcting himself)**  
I think I said that wrong. Sorry. I meant—  I meant *“I’d like to leave now.”*

**The anchor, utterly stone-faced, nods once.**

**ANCHOR**  
Yes.  We would like that too.

**Jim stares at the camera.**

**JIM (in English, under his breath)**  
God, just strike me dead on the air. Give me the ratings at least.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Next Question” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:43 A.M. – SBS LIVE BROADCAST, SOUTH KOREA**

The **South Korean anchor** stares coldly through the screen. The accusation hangs there: *Was she gang-raped by a basketball team?*

**Jim** closes his eyes for half a beat, then opens them. Steady.  He speaks with crisp, measured authority — dead tired, **but not dead inside.**

**JIM (clear, flat)**  
No.

**He lets it hang for half a second.**

**JIM**  
She was **not** gang-raped by a basketball team.

**Beat.**

**JIM (pointed)**  
*Next question.*

He leans forward, elbows on the desk.

**JIM (tight smile)**  
And please…*make it a good one.*

**The anchor adjusts his glasses, suddenly unsure.**

**JIM (softer, but firm)**  
Because I’ve had a long night.  And I’m still speaking to you with respect.  Let’s try to keep it that way.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Break the American” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:47 A.M. – SBS LIVE BROADCAST, SOUTH KOREA**

**Jim** has just shut down the “basketball team” question with poise.  But the anchor doesn’t flinch. If anything — he **smiles** wider.

**ANCHOR (in perfect English, with a slow nod)**  
Ah, I see. My apologies.  *American sensibilities.* Very delicate.

**Jim raises an eyebrow.**

**ANCHOR (leaning forward)**  
You seem tense, Jim-ssi.  Would you describe yourself as *morally exhausted*,  or simply *ashamed*?

**Jim blinks. He clocks it now — the shift in energy.**  **This isn’t a misunderstanding.  This is *intentional.*

**ANCHOR (deadpan)**  
NHK had the footage first.  You must feel very small in your office right now.  Would you like to confess something to my viewers?

**Jim (flat, in his head)**  
Oh, he’s trying to go viral.  He wants the American to break on-air.  He’s not just broadcasting — he’s *hunting.*

**Out loud, Jim straightens. Composure locked.**

**JIM (icy calm)**  
I’m not ashamed.  And I’m not here to make your headline.  I’m here to protect a woman who nearly died.  If that disappoints your producers, you’ll have to live with that.

**A beat. The anchor smiles faintly.**

**ANCHOR**  
Well said.

**Jim nods. Once.**

**JIM (quieter)**  
You’re not gonna break me, my friend.  So maybe ask something useful.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Suddenly, I’m Hungry” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – SBS LIVE BROADCAST, 2:51 A.M.**

The South Korean anchor stares at Jim, waiting for the next crack to show.  But Jim smiles.  Not politely. Not nervously. But **predatory** — the kind of grin you flash right before you sink your teeth into the story *they* were trying to write about you.

**JIM (cool, with bite)**  
*Gapjagi baega gopeuda.*

**The anchor blinks. Once.**

**JIM (still smiling)**  
Suddenly, I’m hungry.

**He leans in, voice calm and razor-sharp.**

**JIM**  
So unless your next question comes with kimchi and clarity, I suggest we wrap this little performance art session up.

**The anchor sits very still. A flicker of something — maybe respect, maybe rage — passes over his face.**

**ANCHOR (tight smile)**  
Americans are becoming more fluent.

**JIM (smiling)**  
In survival?  We invented it.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Pull the Pin” – SBS Seoul Studio / Split-Screen Broadcast**

**INT. SOUTH KOREAN NEWSROOM – LIVE BROADCAST**

The Korean anchor stares at Jim through the monitor, watching the American’s smug little “suddenly I’m hungry” grin.

**INTERNAL MONOLOGUE – ANCHOR**

**ANCHOR (in his head)**  
Alright, fine.  You want to play this game, Jim-ssi?  Let’s see what you do when the floor gives out.

**ANCHOR (cold, quiet inside)**  
I did **two years** of military service.  I’ve thrown real grenades.  Cleaned live rounds.  Slept next to C4.  *You think your sarcasm scares me?*

He adjusts his tie. Voice smooth as glass.

**ANCHOR (thinking)**  
Let’s pull the pin.

Out loud:

**ANCHOR (smiling faintly)**  
Jim-ssi…

**Beat.**

**ANCHOR (measured, lethal)**  
Do you believe Ms. Lavigne *wanted to die* that night?

**Silence.**

The question detonates.  **On Jim’s face — just the smallest flicker of tension.**  Because that?  **Was the grenade.**

---

# **: “…and They Are Ours” – Side Office, Island Records**

**INT. SMALL OFFICE – 2:56 A.M. – FINAL MOMENTS OF THE SBS INTERVIEW**

The question hits like a slap:  **“Do you believe Ms. Lavigne wanted to die that night?”** Jim doesn’t take the bait — **he contemplates torching the whole fucking stage.**  The anchor thought he was tossing a grenade.  Jim?  He pulled a *nuke* out of his back pocket.  This is **midwestern rage meets global burnout**, wrapped in one *final, iconic act of defiance*. He gave the guy a chance. He played nice. He stayed calm under fire. And now? Jim’s done being professional.  

**He’s going out like a legend. He calculates.**

**JIM (in his head)**  
Alright. You want shock? You want your scoop?  **Here’s your goddamn clip.**

He stares dead into the camera, expression flat, voice low.

**JIM (aloud, sharp)**  
*자위해.*  
(*Jawihae.*)

He says it slow. On purpose. Let it land.  The anchor’s eyes widen — he **knows**. The control room knows.  The **millions watching**? They absolutely know.  **And Jim smiles. The kind of smile you give when you're dousing a dumpster fire with lighter fluid.**

**JIM**  
*Ohio versus the world.*  It never changes, baby.

**He flips the bird.**  **And ends the call.**

**Thirty seconds later**, the clip’s already being cut, subtitled, memed.

**\#Jawihae**  
**\#OhioVersusTheWorld**  
**#PRMeltdownLegend**

Jim didn’t break under pressure.  He **became the machine press**.

---

### **SCENE: “Stepped In It” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. ELEVATOR – EARLY MORNING**

The elevator hums quietly as it ascends to the 14th floor.

**Jim** leans against the back wall, tie loosened, eyes locked on nothing.

**JIM (to himself, low)**  
Okay.  So… Maybe I just set back U.S.-Korean relations to 1951.

**DING.**

The doors slide open.

---

**INT. ISLAND RECORDS – CONFERENCE ROOM – CONTINUOUS**

The room is dim. Most of the team is still in various states of collapse — **Cremeans half-asleep at his laptop**, **Sarah groaning into her coffee**, **Jeff and Jeremy arguing over nothing**.

The glass doors open.  **Jim steps in.**  He walks in slowly, like a man who just emerged from the jungle.  Stops at the head of the table.

**JIM (loudly, flatly)**  
*Guys…*

**They all turn. Groggy. Suspicious. Dreading.**

**JIM (dead serious)**  
…I may have just **stepped in it.**

**Silence.**

**JEFF (blinking)**  
How deep are we talkin’?

**JIM**  
Korean War. 1950s. DMZ type shit.

**SARAH (muttering into her mug)**  
Please tell me you didn’t say anything obscene in Korean.

**JIM (quietly, with regret and pride in equal parts)**  
…It was fluent.

**CREMEANS (waking up fully)**  
Oh no.  Oh *no*.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “It’s All In the Delivery” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 14TH FLOOR – MOMENTS LATER**

The team is staring at Jim like he just came back from committing a minor war crime.

**SARAH (groaning)**  
We’re all going to die, aren’t we?

**JIM (nodding solemnly)**  
Probably.

**Everyone tenses. Waiting.**

**JEREMY (nervous)**  
Okay, just… what *exactly* did you say?

**JIM (casual, like he’s naming a breakfast cereal)**  
*Jawihae.*

**Blank stares. A beat.**

**CREMEANS (frowning)**  
That sounds… modest. Like… herbal?

**JEFF (shrugs)**  
Could be a soft drink.

**JIM (calmly)**  
Yeah, it does. Until you say it at the **exact right moment**, with the **exact right delivery**, on **live Korean television**, to a guy who just implied your artist was suicidal and you were covering it up.

**Beat.**

**JIM (smiling faintly)**  
Then it means: *“Go jerk off, asshole.”*

**Silence.**

**SARAH (blinking slowly)**  
Oh… Jesus.

**JEREMY (whispering)**  
He said it *fluently*?

**CREMEANS (closing his laptop)**  
We’re getting nuked.

**JIM (sipping someone’s abandoned coffee)**  
Hey. I used the honorific form.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “234 Videos Later” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

**Cremeans** hits “play” on one of **234** YouTube uploads that just appeared in the last 90 seconds. The screen shows **Jim** on live Korean TV, leaning into the camera with that wild, dangerous smile.

**ON SCREEN:**

**JIM (dead serious)**  
*Jawihae.*  *Ohio versus the world. It never changes, baby.*

**Then — the middle finger.**  **And the feed cuts.**

**SARAH (watching, slack-jawed)**  
Jim…

**She turns to him slowly.**

**SARAH (dry as hell)**  
You *left out* the part about flipping off the camera.  And your macho *“Ohio versus the world”* moment.  

*Shit.*

**Beat.**

**JIM (leaning back, unfazed)**  
What’s your point?

**SARAH (exhausted)**  
My point is we're gonna need a second lawyer, a media firm with bulletproof glass, and maybe a prayer circle.

**JIM (sips the coffee again)**  
Add some Waffle House and I’ll call it a win.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Korean Twitter Loves Him” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MINUTES LATER**

**Cremeans** is doomscrolling. **Sarah** is swearing softly into her palm. **Jeremy’s head is in his hands.**  
And **Jeff** is calmly scrolling his phone, blinking like he just found out Santa’s real.

**JEFF (almost surprised)**  
Well…*Korean Twitter is blown up.*

Everyone looks up.

**JEFF (shrugs)**  
*Uniformly positive.*

**SARAH (disbelieving)**  
What?

**JEFF (reading aloud)**  
“American PR man refuses to be humiliated by bad-faith journalist. Flips bird. Speaks fluent Korean. Respects women. National hero.”  Four thousand retweets.

**JIM (frowning)**  
That’s not… what happened.

**JEFF (grinning)**  
Doesn’t matter. It’s the *legend* now.

**SARAH** just stares at the ceiling.

**JEREMY (quietly)**  
They *like* him?

**JEFF**  
Apparently they love the way he said it.  Someone said it sounded like their *grandpa telling off a scammer.*

**Beat.**

**JEFF (deadpan)**  
Probably the accent.

**JIM (after a pause, smugly)**  
Ohio, baby.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Manhwa? Seriously?” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

Everyone is still reeling from the *"Jim is beloved in Korea now"* twist.  **Jeff** is still scrolling, stunned.  **Jim** is leaning back, smug.  **Sarah** is rubbing her temples.  Then, from the couch — barely awake, voice low:

**BILL (flat)**  
And these are the people that brought us *Manhwa*?

**A beat. Silence.**

**JEREMY (half-laughs)**  
Yup.

**CREMEANS (nodding)**  
Makes total sense now.

**JIM (grinning)**  
Plot twist, baby.

**SARAH (under her breath)**  
I need a drink. And maybe a passport.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “No More Languages” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – CONTINUOUS**

The team is still processing that Jim somehow became **a viral hero** for telling off a Korean anchor in fluent profanity.

**Sarah**, sitting upright now, eyes bloodshot but clear, looks around the table with the slow intensity of a teacher calling roll after a food fight.

**SARAH (flat)**  
Okay.  Quick show of hands.

**She raises her hand slightly. Everyone else watches, wary.**

**SARAH**  
Does anybody here speak…  **Hindi? Arabic? Urdu? Farsi? Swahili? Amharic?**

**Silence. Not a twitch.**

**JEREMY** looks at the floor like it might have answers.  **Jeff** pretends to check his phone.  **Bill** just raises one eyebrow like, *“Lady, you know better.”*

**SARAH (nods slowly)**  
…*Thank fuck.*

**Beat.**

**SARAH (more to herself)**  
Because I was *desperately* trying to avoid someone else creating a scenario that would instantly cause **World War III**.

**CREMEANS (deadpan)**  
We’ll limit our disasters to three time zones per day.

**JIM (mock salute)**  
Yes, ma’am. Back to English. Land of lawsuits and mild disappointment.

---

# **“Caffeine Oracle” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

**JEFF (groaning, head in hands)**  
Dammit.  Getting a splitting migraine.  Like an angry dwarf swinging an axe between my eyes.

From across the room, *THUNK* — a cold **can of Mountain Dew Code Red** slides across the table with surgical accuracy, landing right in front of Jeff.

**CREMEANS (barely looking up from his laptop)**  
Caffeine.  Vasoconstriction.  Neuroinflammation reduction.  Science, baby.

**JEFF (blinking)**  
…You just keep this stuff around?

**CREMEANS (grinning)**  
Island stocks the fridge when I’m in town.  Right next to the Perrier and the bad decisions.

**JEFF (cracking the can)**  
This isn’t a cry for help?

**CREMEANS**  
It’s a cry for performance.  That’s **Code Red**, by the way — the nuclear option.  Sip carefully or you’ll start seeing colors in fourth dimensions.

**JEFF (sipping, grimacing)**  
Jesus. That’s violent.

**CREMEANS (proudly)**  
So am I.

**SARAH (dryly)**  
You’re the only human I know who treats Mountain Dew like medication.

**CREMEANS (pointing to the can)**  
That’s not *a* Mountain Dew.  That’s *my IV line.*

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “The Belly Wars” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – SAME MOMENT**

**Cremeans** is leaning back, draining the last of his Code Red like it’s holy nectar.  **Jeff** is halfway through his can.  **Sarah** is not impressed.

**BILL (grumbling, pointing at Cremeans)**  
It’s been like this with this simpleton for, oh Jesus… *thirty years now?*

**He squints.**  

**BILL**  
And look at that *beer belly* you’re hauling around there, Cremeans.

**CREMEANS (doesn’t flinch, grins proudly)**  
Oh no no, sir.

**He pats it like a prize hog.**

**CREMEANS**  
That’s not a *beer belly*.  That’s a **Mountain Dew belly**.  *Every can tells a story.*

**JEREMY (smiling)**  
What’s it say? “Do not operate heavy machinery?”

**CREMEANS (pointing to his gut)**  
It says: *“This body built three number-one albums, a crisis management war room, and a digital bot army in four hours flat.”*

**BILL (muttering)**  
Goddamn living war crime, you are.

**CREMEANS (saluting with the empty can)**  
And proud of it, Grandpa.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Morning Miles” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – EARLY MORNING LIGHT NOW FILTERING IN**

The room is slowly reanimating.  **Cremeans** is cracking open his third Dew.  **Sarah** is combing through her phone like it’s a battlefield report.  **Jeff** is still in Code Red-induced disbelief.

**Jeremy** stands, stretching his back, flexing his shoulders with a slow sigh.

**JEREMY (to no one in particular)**  
Where’s the gym now?

**Everyone looks up.**

**JEREMY (half to himself)**  
Since they renovated the building.  Used to be on six. Or four?

**He grabs his phone and towel from the corner.**

**JEREMY (grumbling)**  
I gotta run.  I need the motion. I need the burn.  It’s gonna be another *miserable* day.

**SARAH (without looking up)**  
You're just figuring that out now?

**JEREMY (heading to the door)**  
Better I’m miserable in a tank top than in this room.

**CREMEANS (calls out)**  
If you collapse on the treadmill, I call dibs on your Spotify login.

**JEREMY (deadpan)**  
If I collapse, play “Bittersweet Symphony” and call my wife.

**Door closes behind him.**

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Punch Drunk Wizard” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

**Cremeans** is pacing like a rat in a Red Bull lab experiment, wired to the moon. **Jeff** is watching him with increasing concern.

**CREMEANS (pointing at the wall)**  
“Bittersweet Symphony” is why we don’t do samples.  Yeah. That. And your mama’s fat.

**Everyone pauses.**

**JEFF (blinks slowly)**  
Okay…You’re done.  You’re officially *done*.

**Cremeans spins around, eyes twitching, still gripping an empty Mountain Dew can like it’s a live grenade.**

**JEFF (gentle but firm)**  
Hey, man. You’re punch drunk. You’ve been up what, 36 hours? Forty?

**CREMEANS (squints)**  
I have not punched any drinks.

**JEFF** stands, walks over, and gently guides Cremeans by the shoulder toward the couch.

**JEFF**  
Time to nap, buddy. Just a short one.  You’re starting to sound like a *subreddit on bath salts*.

**CREMEANS (mumbling)**  
I’m fine… I’m fine… my brain’s just buffering.

**JEFF (softly)**  
Exactly.

**Cremeans collapses onto the couch, still muttering about sync licenses and snack foods. He’s out in thirty seconds.**

**SARAH (without looking up)**  
Finally. Jesus. Somebody shut down the Dew server.

**JEFF (returning to his seat)**  
He’ll be back in twenty minutes.  Like a caffeinated phoenix.

---

# **“Initial Findings” – Bellevue Hospital, NYPD Liaison Room**

**INT. HOSPITAL CONSULTATION ROOM – 4:49 A.M.**

**Fluorescent lighting. Two chairs.  One clipboard.  Tension thick enough to draw and quarter a traitor.**

**DR. SHAW**, early 50s, quietly competent, trauma-seasoned. No dramatics — just precise clinical language.

Across from him: **DETECTIVE RAMOS**, late 40s, from the Special Victims Unit. Staten Island accent. Not here for drama either — just *truth* and *chains of custody*.

**DR. SHAW (even tone)**  
Patient presented with poly-substance intoxication.  Confirmed presence of **cocaine, amphetamine, methamphetamine, and a BAC of 0.23**.  There were also **three distinct semen samples**, all non-matching.  One additional sample found **in her stomach contents**.

**RAMOS (scribbling, tight voice)**  
Three inside? One oral?

**DR. SHAW (nods once)**  
Correct.  There are also signs of **vaginal tearing**.  Some fresh.  Some dating back… possibly 24 to 48 hours.

**A beat.**

**DR. SHAW**  
We’ve documented and preserved everything. Clothing’s bagged. Chain of custody intact.  You’ll get full copies.  But from a medical standpoint?  This wasn’t consensual.

**RAMOS (quiet, jaw flexing)**  
Any needle marks?

**DR. SHAW**  
Yes. Recent. Left forearm. Intravenous.  We also recovered a used syringe from her pocket. Glove sealed and transferred to forensics.

**RAMOS (closing his notebook)**  
So we’ve got a potentially incapacitated woman…Multiple foreign DNA sources…and an abandoned subway station.  That's a hell of a start on a jigsaw puzzle.

**DR. SHAW**  
Correct.

**RAMOS (sighs)**  
Jesus Christ.

**DR. SHAW**  
That’s what I said when I saw the labs.

**Beat.**

**RAMOS (stands)**  
Alright.  Time to call the ADA.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “It’s Already Out There” – Bellevue Hospital**

**INT. HOSPITAL CONSULTATION ROOM – 4:53 A.M.**

**Dr. Shaw** is closing his folder. **Detective Ramos** is standing, ready to contact the ADA.

Suddenly—  **A nurse in scrubs** rushes in, phone in hand, eyes wide.

**NURSE (urgent)**  
Dr. Shaw. You gotta see this.

**SHAW (flat)**  
We’re in the middle of—

**NURSE (interrupts, showing phone)**  
No, you *have to*. It’s on the **frickin’ internet**.  It’s *Avril*.  NHK aired **surveillance footage**.

**Ramos turns sharply. Shaw takes the phone.**

**ON SCREEN: A YouTube video.**  Clip from NHK. **Low-res night-vision surveillance footage.**  Avril — alone — **descending a staircase** into a dimly lit access corridor.

*Timestamped. Labeled: “Entry: 1:07 A.M.”*

She moves unsteadily, but there's **no coercion. No one else in frame.**  Then, **cut to live footage**: Jim in the NHK studio, pale and still.

**ANCHOR (on-screen)**  
*“Does this alter your position, Jim-ssi? Did she intend to descend into danger?”*

**JIM (voice like flint)**  
*“Jawihae.”*  *“Ohio versus the world. It never changes, baby.”*  *[Middle finger. Cut feed.]*

**SHAW (blinking)**  
Christ almighty.

**NURSE (softly)**  
It’s at **2.6 million views**. Trending in Korea, Japan, and now here.  Somebody deep-translated it in *thirteen* languages.  People are already picking sides.

**RAMOS (jaw tightens)**  
So now we've got a patient with **a full medical trauma profile**…and a **broadcast clip that paints her as voluntarily entering the scene.**

**SHAW (exhaling hard)**  
And a media rep who just told the Eastern Hemisphere to go masturbate. On camera.

**RAMOS**  
I’m calling the ADA.

**SHAW (deadpan)**  
And I’m calling legal.  This just got radioactive.

---

### **SCENE SNIPPET: “I Thought He Was the Drummer” – Bellevue, Hallway Outside the Consultation Room**

**INT. HOSPITAL HALLWAY – MOMENTS AFTER**

**Detective Ramos** is already dialing the ADA.  **Dr. Shaw** is halfway through composing a legal escalation email.  The nurse from earlier lingers outside the room, still holding her phone.

Beside her, **a younger orderly**, maybe mid-20s, leans in, watching the Jim video loop again.

**ORDERLY (tilting his head)**  
Man’s got a *way* with words.

**NURSE (nodding)**  
Yeah… I thought he was the drummer.

**ORDERLY**  
What?

**NURSE (shrugs)**  
Jim. The guy in the video.  Totally thought he was just the band’s drummer.

**ORDERLY (genuine)**  
Same. He’s got drummer vibes.

**They watch the middle finger freeze-frame.**

**ORDERLY**  
I mean… it *feels* like a drummer move.

**NURSE**  
Yeah. But apparently, he’s the PR guy, too.

**ORDERLY (beat)**  
Jesus. That’s worse.

---

# **“Are We Banned Yet?” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:02 A.M.**

**Cremeans** is snoring softly in the corner, curled up like a passed-out goblin king.  The room is dim. The Mountain Dew fridge hums. Phones buzz occasionally with **foreign language push notifications**.  **Jeff** stares blankly at a Twitter trending chart he doesn’t understand.

**JEFF (murmuring)**  
You think we’ll ever get to play in Seoul again?

**JEREMY (shrugs)**  
I like gimbap.  I like bulgogi.  I like playing in Korea.

**JEFF**  
Korean baseball’s pretty cool too.

**They pause. Sip. Stare into nothing.**

**SARAH (flat, from across the room)**  
I don’t believe you assholes.

**JEREMY (shrugs again)**  
What? It *is* cool. They do the songs. Choreographed chants.  It’s like baseball with a plot.

**JEFF**  
Better than Cleveland.

**SARAH (rubbing her eyes)**  
You’re all insane.

**CREMEANS (from the couch, half-asleep)**  
Bulgogi has protein. It’s good for recovery.

**SARAH (quietly to herself)**  
I need a new job. Preferably in data entry.

---

### **SCENE SNIPPET: “Rated: Please No” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:08 A.M.**

**Cremeans** is snoring again.  **Sarah** is hunched over her laptop, deleting drafts of press releases she’ll never send.  **Jeff** is trying to Google “damage control in Korean.”  **Jeremy** is scrolling through fan memes of Jim.

And then—

**SARAH (suddenly, dead serious)**  
This transcript contains material not suitable for minors under 18.

**Beat.**

**SARAH (louder)**  
This transcript contains material not suitable for minors under **forty-five**.

**Silence.**

**JEREMY (quietly)**  
…She’s not wrong.

**CREMEANS (half-conscious)**  
Add a surgeon general warning. And a trigger warning. And a *parental advisory sticker from 1997\.*

**JEFF (sipping his Dew)**  
Just brand it with a skull and a middle finger.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “New Outlook Energy” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:09 A.M.**

The room is quiet again. **Cremeans** has devolved into soft, rhythmic mumbling.  **Jeff** is refreshing Twitter for news he’s not ready to read.  **Jeremy** is typing with two fingers like a caveman.  **Sarah** closes her laptop slowly, like she’s sealing a coffin.

**SARAH (softly, to no one in particular)**  
I just might make that my new signature block in Outlook.

---

### **SCENE: “The Scan” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:26 A.M.**

The lights are dim. The air is stale.  Somebody’s phone buzzes and nobody even flinches.  **Cremeans stirs on the couch.**  **Rubs his face.**  **Sits up.**  **Cold reboot complete.**  He squints at the room.  One by one, **he scans them** like a general surveying the aftermath of a firefight.

**CREMEANS (internal monologue, or maybe just under his breath):**

Evans the elder: completely fallen apart.  Malcolm: dangerously dangling off the cliff.  Evans the younger: ran away in gym shorts, probably hiding from his own inbox.  And Bill…

His eyes land on **Bill Davenport**, seated quietly, arms crossed, **utterly unreadable**.

**CREMEANS (quietly)**  
…Bill looks like he watched the building burn down and decided to move in anyway.

**Beat.**

**CREMEANS (rubbing his temples)**  
Jesus Christ.  This room’s got the energy of a dead zoo.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Stand Down Orders” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:30 A.M.**

Cremeans stands fully now, back straight, energy centered. The band and Sarah look up — barely — like burnt-out soldiers hearing a new command after too long in the trench.

**CREMEANS (voice flat but firm)**  
Alright. Everybody shut up and listen.  I’m getting **all of you** a hotel room.  **That includes you, Sarah** — because unless you want to drive the wrong way down the Long Island Expressway at 6 A.M., that’s a death wish.

**He walks to the table, phone already out, thumbs flying.**

**CREMEANS**  
I’m calling Ubers. Everyone gets one. You get in. You sleep. You **don’t** open social media.

**He looks around the room like a drill sergeant doing headcount.**

**CREMEANS**  
We meet back here at **2 PM**. No earlier.  None of you are making sense.  We are not doing ourselves any favors.

**A beat. His voice darkens.**

**CREMEANS**  
When the lawyer gets here, **he and I** will handle it.  It’s going to be unpleasant. It’s going to be awful. It’s going to be terrible.  But we will do what we have to do.

**He turns toward the door, then stops.**

**CREMEANS**  
*Mattie*, that goes for you too.  You don’t go home. You get a room. You rest. Full stop.

**JEFF (soft correction)**  
That’s *Madeline*, sir.  Madeline. *Underline it.*

**CREMEANS (pauses, nods once without looking back)**  
Then underline it in red.  Because she doesn’t go home either.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Permission to Exhale” – Island Records, Conference Room**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**

The room is quiet now.  No shouting.  No snark.  Just the low hum of a fridge full of Mountain Dew.  **Sarah** crosses slowly to the oversized leather chair in the corner — the one no one ever sits in unless they’ve truly had enough.  She drops into it.  Heavy. Final.

**SARAH**  (sighs)  
God.

She tilts her head back, stares at the ceiling and closes her eyes.  Not quite  But for the first time in hours —  **she’s not bracing for impact.**

---

### **SCENE: “Exit Sequence” – Island Records, Morning Break**

**INT. CONFERENCE ROOM – 5:45 A.M.**

Silence.  Just the distant city hum below.  Phones buzz with ride confirmations. No one reacts.  **Jeff** stands first, sluggish, rubbing his temples.  He doesn’t say goodbye.  He just walks toward the elevator.  **Jeremy** follows, earbuds in, hoodie up. Still hasn’t stopped running — just paused for a few hours.

**Bill** doesn’t speak. Doesn’t blink.  Just picks up his jacket, slings it over one shoulder, and moves like a shadow.  **Sarah**, still in the big leather chair, finally exhales.  She opens her eyes.  Then stands.

Last is **Cremeans**, phone still in hand, scanning the rides, verifying destinations.  He watches them go.

---

**INT. ELEVATOR – MOMENTS LATER**

Each one steps in alone or in pairs.  No words. Just the soft **ding** of descending steel and fluorescent silence.

---

**EXT. ISLAND RECORDS – EARLY MORNING**

Ubers idle along the curb.  One by one, they emerge, climb in, and vanish into the **softly brightening sunlight** that spills through the concrete canyons of Manhattan.  The sky is a pale promise.  Another day.  Another storm.  But for now?  **They disappear into the glow.**

---

# **“Sell Me” – Bellevue Hospital, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. PRIVATE CONSULT ROOM – 6:45 A.M.**

**Assistant District Attorney Marcus Reyes**, mid-40s, stone face, immaculate suit, steps into the room. He’s already read **four conflicting reports**, seen **one trending video**, and taken **two calls from the mayor’s office**.

Seated before him:

* **Detective Ramos**, SVU.
* **Dr. Shaw**, trauma physician.
* **A hospital legal rep.**

**REYES (voice flat)**  
Alright. Someone walk me through this.  Not what happened. Not what you *think* happened.  Tell me what I can take into a courtroom.

**Ramos starts.**  **Shaw interjects.**  A flurry of details spill out—

Three semen samples.  Torn clothing.  Vaginal tearing.  No visible bruises.  No broken bones.  No significant skin or flesh under the nails.  No defensive wounds.  Syringe. Drugs.  A surveillance video of her entering the site alone.

**REYES (holding up a hand)**  
Stop!  

So: we’ve got circumstantial trauma, but no clear force.  No screaming. No direct witness.  Ripped clothes, yes. But no broken ribs. No skull fracture. No choke bruising.

**Beat.**  

**REYES**  
But we have tearing. And we have drugs.  And we have multiple men.

**Ramos nods. Shaw nods. The room is quiet.**

**REYES (cold now)**  
You tell me.  Can I walk this into a courtroom in Lower Manhattan— *convince twelve people who live on a diet of Netflix crime docs and TikTok psychobabble* that this woman was raped?

**A longer silence.**

**REYES (soft, brutal)**  
I want you to sell me.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “The Burden of Selling It” – Bellevue, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – 6:47 A.M.**

The silence hangs for a beat after Reyes' challenge: *“Sell me.”*

He doesn’t wait for a response.  He leans forward, drops his voice, and twists the knife.

**ADA REYES (measured, dangerous)**  
Let’s take a breath and consider the context.  You know where Avril Lavigne was found?

**He doesn’t wait.**

**REYES**  
She wasn’t in a hotel suite.  She wasn’t pulled out of a frat house.  She was in **an abandoned subway station** in Alphabet City.  The kind of place that makes Vice documentaries and missing persons cases.

**He lets that sink in.**

**REYES**  
You know what happens in that space?  *That’s where people go to get their freak on.*  Where people go when they don’t want to be found.  When they want to leave the world for a while.  To **exit**, to **descend**, to **practice depravity**.

**Beat. Then the second knife.**

**REYES (darker now)**  
Now let’s talk about her behavior this past week.  Do we need to go over the videos again?  Do we need to hear her say what she said in that *back alley with Jacques*?  Do I need to pull the frame-by-frame breakdown of her Instagram Stories?  **Fifty-three nude selfies.**  **Two hours of public footage** of her either having sex, masturbating, drinking, snorting, smoking — all of it posted *by her*.  She’s been live-streaming her spiral for six days.

**He pauses. Breathes. Then throws down the hammer.**

**REYES (quiet and sharp)**  
You tell me.  You **sell me**.  You convince me that this woman is a victim —  **and not the defense attorney’s dream witness for a consensual gangbang gone bad.**

**Another long silence.**

**REYES**  
Because if you can’t sell me now, I sure as hell can’t sell it to a jury in Lower Manhattan.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “She Went Through Hell” – Bellevue, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – MOMENTS AFTER**

Reyes has just finished his ruthless challenge:  *“You tell me this woman is a victim.”*

Silence.

Then — from her chair — **Detective Ramos** finally speaks.

**RAMOS (even, grounded)**  
She went through hell.

**All heads turn. Reyes doesn’t flinch.**

**RAMOS**  
You want to talk about context, ADA Reyes?  Here’s context.  I’ve seen the evidence.  I’ve looked at her myself.  She wasn’t just drunk. She wasn’t just high.  She was **unconscious**, barely breathing, her body torn up inside.

**Beat.**

**RAMOS**  
No bruises? No broken bones?  So what?  What century are we in where that’s the bar for rape?

**Shaw lowers his eyes. The hospital attorney says nothing.**

**RAMOS (sharper now)**  
There were **three different DNA samples inside her.**  There’s **internal tearing**.  There’s **IV drug use**, and no indication she administered it herself.  There’s **footage of her wandering into a place people go to disappear.**

**She steps forward.**

**RAMOS**  
That doesn’t make her complicit.  That makes her a target.  And we don’t get to say, “Oh well, she was spiraling” and wash our hands of it.

**She looks directly at Reyes. Calm. Firm.**

**RAMOS**  
She was raped.  I’m not here to polish a courtroom speech.  I’m here to make sure this woman’s pain isn’t erased because someone thinks she posted too many selfies.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Final Word” – Bellevue, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – MOMENTS AFTER**

Reyes stares at her. No expression.  The air is thick. The kind of silence that only follows a truth someone didn’t want to hear.

**Ramos doesn’t blink.  Doesn’t soften.**

**RAMOS (quiet, razor sharp)**  
Fuck you, sir.

She turns, walks out, slow and steady.  Leaves the silence behind her.  Lets it echo.

---

# **“Boiling Point” – Bellevue Hospital, Main Break Room**

**INT. HOSPITAL BREAK ROOM – 6:55 A.M.**

The fluorescent lights buzz faintly.  Plastic chairs. Stale granola bars. A humming refrigerator.  A muted **LCD television** plays local news no one’s watching.

**Detective Ramos** storms in.  She doesn’t speak.  Doesn’t grunt.  Doesn’t even take off her jacket.  She walks straight to the counter, grabs the **Keurig coffee maker** —  **still warm, still half-full** —  and with one clean, practiced motion, **hurls it across the room.**

**CRASH.**

The Keurig hits the television **dead center.**The LCD **shatters**, screen bursting into static as the unit **rips from the wall**, slamming to the floor with a hollow **thud** and a pop of **burnt plastic and sparks.**The break room is now completely silent.  Only the sound of the Keurig’s water tank **dripping onto tile.**

**Ramos exhales.**  **Once.**  **Long.**And walks out.

---

### **SCENE: “Sword and Shield” – Manhattan Subway, Early Morning**

**INT. SUBWAY STAIRS – 7:05 A.M.**

**Detective Ramos** moves fast.  Down the stairs. Through the crowd.  Doesn’t look at anyone. Doesn’t need to.  Her jaw is tight.  Her fists are still half-clenched.  Her badge weighs heavier today.

And in her head, the rant rolls.

**RAMOS (V.O.)**  
It’s always the same goddamn thing. They   stand there in suits. With pens. And folders.  And call it **the law**.

They say *“We need more evidence.”*  *“We need to be sure.”*  *“We need to protect the system.”*

What they really mean is **protect themselves**.  They use the Constitution like a goddamn riot shield.  Not to defend the weak —  **to block the truth.**  They say it’s about **burden of proof**.  But somehow, the burden’s always on the girl who bled in the dark and can’t remember which hand held her down first.  They say they’re upholding the law.  But most days, it just feels like they’re **delaying justice until it gives up and goes home.**

---

**INT. SUBWAY PLATFORM – CONTINUOUS**

The train roars in.  **Ramos** steps inside.  Doesn’t sit. Just stands.  Eyes forward. Breath steady.  Still seething.  Still thinking.  Still ready to fight.

---

# **“What's Going On, Doctor?” – Bellevue Hospital, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – 7:08 A.M.**

The room is still.  The echo of **Ramos's departure** and the crash from the break room still hangs in the air.  The Keurig incident hasn’t been mentioned.  No one dares.  **ADA Reyes** straightens the stack of reports in front of him like he’s trying to put the universe back in order.  He looks at **Dr. Shaw**, deadpan.

**REYES (dryly)**  
Well… That was about as productive as watching the Titanic sink.

**He exhales. Sharp. Measured.**  

**REYES**  
What’s going on, Doctor?

**He locks eyes with Shaw.**

**REYES**  
Medically. Clinically. Real-world.  Not politics.  Not pain.  Just… *your opinion*.  What happened to that woman?

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Clinical Clarity” – Bellevue Hospital, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – 7:09 A.M.**

Dr. Shaw adjusts his glasses. The air is brittle.  No one says a word.

**SHAW (measured, clinical)**  
I reiterate; medically speaking… What we have is a **poly-substance-intoxicated female**, presenting with:

* Three distinct **seminal DNA samples** present in vaginal, cervical, and rectal cavities.
* **Vaginal tearing** consistent with rough intercourse — possible penetration by multiple partners.
* **No visible external bruising.**
* **No fractures.**
* **No defensive wounds.**
* Minimal biological trace material under fingernails.
* Positive for **IV drug use**, recent injection site on left antecubital.

**He pauses. No one interrupts.**

**SHAW (continued)**  
Clothing was torn, but pattern does not suggest violent stripping — no linear stretch marks, no handprint bruising.  No signs of restraint.  Pupils were unresponsive. She was nonverbal.  Toxicology: cocaine, methamphetamine, amphetamine, and alcohol — BAC 0.23.

**He exhales once, just enough.**

**SHAW**  
Put simply:  She was **deeply impaired**.  She was **used**.  But the clinical evidence **does not show resistance**.  It does not show a struggle.  It shows… *access*.

**He finally looks at Reyes.**

**SHAW (softly, but final)**  
It doesn’t mean she wasn’t raped.  It just means it’s going to be **very hard to prove that she was.**

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “No Rush to Judgment” – Bellevue Hospital, Legal Consult Room**

**INT. CONSULT ROOM – 7:12 A.M.**

The room is still after Dr. Shaw's grim assessment.  **ADA Marcus Reyes** closes the file in front of him slowly.  Not dramatically — just final. His voice is calm, deliberate.

**REYES**  
Under the law, every person is presumed innocent until proven guilty by a jury of their peers.

**He looks around the room, then at Shaw.**

**REYES (measured)**  
It is my job — *our job* — to ensure that **justice** is done.  Not vengeance.  Not noise.  **Justice.**

**He stands now. Controlled. Tired. But resolute.**

**REYES**  
Given the complexity of this case, the ambiguity of the evidence, and the public volatility already building…I’m going to recommend to the District Attorney — and to my supervisor —  that we **sit on this** for the time being.  No charges. No statement. No move.

**Beat.**

**REYES (firmer)**  
Because anything we do here —  in the dark, this early, with this little information —  wouldn’t be justice.  It would be **a catastrophic miscarriage of it**.

**He adjusts his coat.**

**REYES**  
And I won't be the one who blows this case before it’s even built.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Political Animal” – Bellevue Hospital, Legal Consult Room**

The room stays quiet after Reyes’s measured conclusion.  No objections. No applause.  Just… tension.  Then a voice — dry, bitter, just loud enough to land.

**UNKNOWN FEMALE VOICE (maybe Shaw, maybe the hospital legal)**  
You sound like you’re signing up for a run at a Senate seat, **you son of a bitch.**

**Reyes doesn't flinch. He just picks up his folder and says nothing.**  Because maybe he is.  And maybe he knows it.

---

### **SCENE: “Shift Change” – Bellevue ICU, Early Morning**

**INT. INTENSIVE CARE UNIT – 7:30 A.M.**

The hum of machines.  The soft beep of monitors.  The smell of bleach and processed air.  **A new set of nurses** has taken over.  Fresh scrubs. Fresh coffee. But already emotionally tired.  They gather around the chart at **Room 217**.  The name is there: *Avril Lavigne.*  The vitals are there too — and they tell a different story.

**NURSE #1 (scanning chart)**  
Jesus.

**NURSE #2 (reading the file)**  
Three semen samples.  Full tox panel. Amphetamines, coke, meth, ethanol.  IV injection site.

**NURSE #3 (quiet)**  
I heard she was underground. Like, subway system, abandoned platform.  They pulled her out just before the rats got to her.

**NURSE #1**  
You’re kidding.

**NURSE #3 (flat)**  
Wish I was.

A beat.

**NURSE #2 (softly)**  
She ever going to wake up?

**NURSE #1 (hesitates, then)**  
Odds are pretty good she **will** today.  But we can’t exclude catatonia either.  She might be… like this for weeks.  Or longer.  Could be forever.

**They stand in silence. Machines beep. Lights blink.**  **The girl in the bed doesn’t move.**

---

# **“The Line We Don’t Cross” – Bellevue ICU, Room 217**

**INT. ICU – 7:36 A.M.**

They’ve moved on from the chart.  Now they’re prepping for a full wound cleanse.

**NURSE #3 (glancing at notes)**  
They had to remove **glass** from her rectal area.

**NURSE #1 (winces)**  
Glass?

**NURSE #3 (nods)**  
Yeah. She **sat on a crack pipe**, apparently.  Microscopic shards.  Some embedded. Some free-floating.

**A quiet pause. No judgment. Just horror.**

**NURSE #2 (softly)**  
Have you actually been… paying attention to all of this?

**She gestures faintly toward the chart. The monitors. The name.**

**NURSE #2 (continued)**  
I think it’d be best if we just…ignored the whole **celebrity** thing.

**NURSE #1 looks over.**

**NURSE #2 (firm now)**  
Because once we start obsessing about that, she stops being the patient.  She becomes **the brand**. **The drama.**  And we stop doing our job.

**Beat. The room falls into a heavy silence.** On the bed, **Avril** doesn’t move.  The machines continue their work.  So do the nurses.

---

### **SCENE: “Lockdown” – Bellevue ICU, Nurses’ Station**

**INT. ICU NURSES' STATION – 7:45 A.M.**

The floor is quiet, but humming.  Monitors flicker. Charts shift. Murmurs of the day shift nurses in rotation.

**The Chief of Nursing** — crisp scrubs, steel in her step — strides out of the elevator like **a weapon drawn**.

**NURSE #1 (whispers)**  
That’s Davis. She just came out of Legal.

**The Chief walks directly into the center of the nurses’ cluster. Doesn’t ask for attention. Just starts.**

**CHIEF DAVIS (flat, clear)**  
Everyone listen.

**The room freezes. She looks each of them in the eye. One by one.**

**CHIEF DAVIS**  
You will keep your mouth shut.  You will respect this patient’s **legal rights**.  You will protect all **identifiable information**.  And by **God** — *HIPAA is a thing.*

**She takes a step closer. Lowering her voice.**

**CHIEF DAVIS**  
If any one of you even thinks about talking—to the press, to your spouse, to your sister, or to a fucking comment section— you will lose your job, your license, and your name.  And these people?  They’ve got lawyers who make **God nervous**.  They will tear your soul apart and **eat it with salt.**

**Beat.**

**CHIEF DAVIS (icier now)**  
No leaks.  You don’t post.  You don’t whisper.  You don’t blink.

**She looks around one more time.**

**CHIEF DAVIS**  
Am. I. Clear?

**A chorus of muted nods.**    **Silence follows her out.**

---

### **SCENE: “The Justification Spiral” – Bellevue ICU, Nurse Station Workroom**

**INT. NURSE STATION WORKROOM – 8:16 A.M.**

**Nurse Amy Geiger**, mid-30s, competent, methodical, is staring at a toxicology summary printout.  **It’s not just a report.**  It’s *her line in the sand.*

**AMY (V.O.)**  
She thinks she can talk to us like that?  Like we’re children?  *“You’ll lose your soul. They’ll eat it with salt.”*  What the hell kind of leadership is that?

**She glares at the closed door where Chief Davis exited.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
First Amendment’s still a thing.  So is *informed public interest*.  This isn’t just some drunk off the street—this is **Avril Lavigne**.  People deserve to know what’s really going on.

**Her eyes drift back to the sheet. The results. The proof.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
They’re hiding this.  The whole damn city’s going to spin it.  Maybe I’m the only one with the spine to stand up and—

**She cuts herself off. Her eyes narrow. She flips over the printout. Then back again.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
Can’t scan it.  Scanners watermark. Microdots.  Printers, too.  Could trace it straight back to me.

**Her jaw tightens.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
What if I just… photograph the report?  Print the photo.  Fax the photo of the printout.  Low-res, no metadata. No fingerprint.

**She stares at the paper. The fax machine. The break room door.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
WABC? Or WikiLeaks?

**She sits. Fumes.**  **Ethics class memories flicker. Privacy lectures. Consent discussions. The phrase *“do no harm.”*** But **the First Amendment keeps flashing louder in her head**.

**AMY (V.O.)**  
She gave up her right to silence when she turned herself into a sideshow.  People need the truth.  They need the truth.

**She stares at the report again. The plan forming.**  **The justifications stacking like dominos.**  And then:  **She pockets the page.**

---

### **SCENE: “Click. Snap. Leak.” – Bellevue ICU, Supply Room**

**INT. SUPPLY ROOM – 8:38 A.M.**

Fluorescent lights. Metal shelves. Sterile silence.  **Nurse Amy Geiger** stands by a rolling med cart, the 43-page toxicology report in front of her, open like a manifesto.

**Page 1. Snap.**  A soft *click* from her phone.  She doesn’t rush.

**Page 2. Snap.**  Perfect angle.  No glare.  No watermark.

**Page 3. Snap.**  Steady hands.  Heartbeat calm.

**AMY (V.O.)**  
Forty-three pages.  Forty-three pieces of truth.

**Page 4. Snap.**  **Page 5. Snap.**  **Page 6. Snap.**

**AMY (V.O.)**  
This’ll teach them.  Three percent raises a year, while Legal drives Teslas.  *We’re the ones in the trenches.*

**Page 7. Snap.**  
**Page 8. Snap.**

**She smiles now. The power is intoxicating.**  **She feels *bigger* than the hospital.**  **Smarter than Davis.**  **Untouchable.**

**Page 9. Snap.**  
**Page 10. Snap.**

---

### **SCENE: “Dropping a Dime” – Bellevue, Then Midtown Manhattan**

**INT. SUPPLY ROOM – 8:40 A.M.**

**Amy Geiger** scrolls through her phone.  **Forty-three images.**  All sharp. All legible. All damning.  She places the original report back into the file tray.  Not a crease out of place.  She straightens her badge.  Wipes the screen.  And exhales.

---

#### **INT. NURSES' STATION – MOMENTS LATER**

**AMY (flatly, to charge nurse)**  
Hey. I’m not feeling great. Migraine.  I’m gonna head out.

**CHARGE NURSE (without looking up)**  
Alright. Logged.

---

#### **EXT. BELLEVUE HOSPITAL – 9:02 A.M.**

Amy walks out into the sunlight like it’s **just another day**.  No rush. No hesitation.

---

#### **INT. FEDEX OFFICE – 9:22 A.M.**

She prints four of the clearest images.  Black and white. Slight blur. No metadata.  Picks up a manila envelope.  Cash, not card.

---

#### **EXT. NEW YORK PUBLIC LIBRARY BRANCH – 9:48 A.M.**

Downstairs. Coin-fed fax machine.  **Five cents a page.**  She feeds them through one by one.

**TOTAL: $2.15**

She doesn’t even take the receipt.

**AMY (V.O.)**  
Justice costs less than a cup of coffee.  And it tastes better, too.

---

### **SCENE: “No Turning Back” – New York Public Library, Branch Basement**

**INT. LIBRARY BASEMENT – 9:52 A.M.**

Fluorescent lights buzz.  A lonely corner with a **coin-operated fax machine** and a dusty information desk.  **Amy Geiger** slides the first of four printed photo pages into the fax tray.  **Destination: A secure, unlisted number traced to a known WikiLeaks drop node.**  **Each page hums through the rollers.**  Buzz. Click. Buzz.  No name. No sender info.  The final page feeds in.  A blinking green light confirms: 

> [!done]
> *SEND COMPLETE.*


Amy removes the pages. Tears them in half. Then into quarters.  Drops the pieces into the trash in six different bins.  **She doesn’t smile.**  **She doesn’t gloat.**  She just picks up her tote bag and walks out of the building like she mailed a birthday card.

**AMY (V.O.)**  
Not a hero.  Not a traitor.  Just tired of silence.

---

# **“Come On Down” – Bellevue Hospital, ICU, Room 217**

**INT. HOSPITAL ROOM – 10:57 A.M.**

A **cardiac monitor** pulses.  A **slow drip** of saline ticks in rhythm.  The **television on the wall**, bolted to the ceiling, hums softly with a pre-show ad for **The Price is Right**.  **Avril Lavigne's eyelids flutter.**  Her pupils dilate.  **She blinks once.**

A nurse notices — quietly leans in, checks vitals.

**AVRIL (V.O., dreamlike)**  
Where…What…

**She tries to speak.**  **Only a rasp escapes.**

**NURSE (gently, professional)**  
You’re in the hospital, Ms. Lavigne.  You’re safe.

**Avril’s eyes shift to the TV.**

**\[DING DING DING\]**  
**“Come on doooown\!”**

**The Price is Right theme begins.**  **A contestant screams.**

**AVRIL (V.O., fractured)**  
No…  No, this isn’t real.  This isn’t how you wake up.

But she’s awake.  Eyes open.  And **her body remembers things she hasn’t yet processed**.

**AVRIL (hoarse)**  
What…  What happened to me?

**NURSE (quiet)**  
You’ve been through something.  We’ll talk soon.  Just rest.

**The Price is Right blares.**  **Applause erupts.**  **Someone wins a washing machine.**  Avril stares at the ceiling.  Breathes in.  Breathes out. Eyes open.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Is Drew Carey God?” – Bellevue ICU, Room 217**

**INT. ROOM 217 – 11:01 A.M.**

**Avril** stares at the television.  Eyes half-lidded. Skin pale. IVs in both arms.  **Drew Carey** smiles brightly from the screen.

*“Showcase Showdown coming up next, folks — don’t go anywhere\!”*  A contestant jumps up and down like they’ve seen the light.

**Avril’s voice croaks, barely audible.**

**AVRIL (raspy, confused)**  
Is…Is Drew Carey God?

**The nurse blinks. Caught off guard.**  **Then just gently presses a hand to Avril’s shoulder.**

**NURSE (softly)**  
No, honey.  But some days I wonder too.

**Avril exhales.**  Not quite a laugh. Not quite a sob.  Something in between.  And the lights above keep humming.

---

### **SCENE: “Just a Simple Question” – Bellevue ICU, Room 217**

**INT. ICU ROOM 217 – 11:04 A.M.**

The **room is dim**, but the **TV is still on**.  Drew Carey is mid-laughter. A woman is screaming over a hot tub package.  
**Avril Lavigne** is conscious.  Eyes unfocused. One wrist **handcuffed to the bedrail**.  

**Enter ALBERT YOUNG**, respiratory tech, 50s, Queens accent, 28 years on the job, zero tolerance for BS.  He walks in with a chart and a tray of tubing.  Stops short at the bed.

**ALBERT (flat, confused)**  
…Okay.  Why the hell is she handcuffed?

**The nurse across the room stiffens. Doesn’t answer immediately.**

**ALBERT (gesturing)**  
She doesn’t look like she’s gonna jump out the window, if you ask me.

**He steps closer, squints at Avril. She blinks at him. Barely present.**

**AVRIL (hoarse)**  
Is… is that God?

**Albert glances at the TV. Drew Carey waves from the screen.**  **Albert snorts.**

**ALBERT**  
If it is, we’re all screwed.

---

### **SCENE CONTINUED: “Move the Bed, Albert” – Bellevue ICU, Room 217**

**INT. ICU ROOM 217 – 11:05 A.M.**

**Albert** stands at the foot of the bed, one eyebrow raised at the handcuff.  **Avril** stares at the ceiling. TV still on.  Drew Carey is describing a jet ski.

**NURSE (calm, rehearsed)**  
She’s being restrained for her own protection.  It’s medical protocol.

**Albert gestures vaguely at the steel cuff.**

**ALBERT**  
Yeah, okay, but that’s a pretty aggressive version of protection.

**NURSE (smiles tightly)**  
And because of medical privacy regulations, that’s *all* you need to know.

**Beat. Albert exhales through his nose, shakes his head a little.**  **This is not the weirdest thing he’s seen.**  **But it’s Top 10\.**

**NURSE (lightly)**  
Would you mind moving the bed about four inches to the left?  We’re going to run O2. Her sats are in the tank.

**ALBERT (grumbling, moving around)**  
Sure. Why not. It’s only Tuesday.  Let me know if she starts levitating.

**He unlocks the wheels.**  **Starts adjusting position.**  **Avril breathes in, shallow and ragged.**

**NURSE (to herself)**  
Let’s see if her brain likes 100% better than 83.

**ALBERT (still shifting the bed)**  
If she starts speaking Latin, I’m outta here.

**NURSE (not missing a beat)**  
Just get the bed lined up, Al.

---

### **SCENE: “Lucid… Ish” – Bellevue ICU, Nurses' Station**

**INT. ICU NURSES’ STATION – 11:09 A.M.**

The nurse who’s been monitoring **Avril** steps away from the room and pulls out her hospital-issued phone.  She dials.

**NURSE (low, calm)**  
Hi, this is ICU — patient 217.  Yeah. Lavigne.

**Pause. Listens.**

**NURSE (measured)**  
She’s awake. Eyes open, responsive, able to speak.

**Another pause.**

**NURSE**  
No. Not lucid.  She’s… talking, but it’s not making sense.

Beat.

She glances through the glass into Avril’s room. **Drew Carey is still smiling on the screen. Avril’s lips are moving slowly.**

**NURSE (dryly)**  
She correctly identified the host of *The Price is Right*, so that’s something.  Unfortunately, she currently believes Drew Carey is God.

**A long pause on the line.  The nurse doesn’t blink.**

**NURSE (bluntly)**  
I’d call it cognitive activity, but not orientation.

**She listens again.**

**NURSE**  
Yeah. Oxygen’s up. We’re monitoring.

**Beat.**

**NURSE (with a touch of gallows humor)**  
If she starts talking to Wayne Brady, I’ll escalate.

---

### **SCENE: “Chart That” – Bellevue ICU, Room 217**

**INT. ICU ROOM 217 – 11:13 A.M.**
